<line act="1" scene="0" line="1" speaker="">In Troy, there lies the scene. From isles of Greece</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="2" speaker="">The princes orgulous, their high blood chafed,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="3" speaker="">Have to the port of Athens sent their ships,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="4" speaker="">Fraught with the ministers and instruments</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="5" speaker="">Of cruel war: sixty and nine, that wore</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="6" speaker="">Their crownets regal, from the Athenian bay</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="7" speaker="">Put forth toward Phrygia; and their vow is made</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="8" speaker="">To ransack Troy, within whose strong immures</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="9" speaker="">The ravish'd Helen, Menelaus' queen,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="10" speaker="">With wanton Paris sleeps; and that's the quarrel.</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="11" speaker="">To Tenedos they come;</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="12" speaker="">And the deep-drawing barks do there disgorge</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="13" speaker="">Their warlike fraughtage: now on Dardan plains</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="14" speaker="">The fresh and yet unbruised Greeks do pitch</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="15" speaker="">Their brave pavilions: Priam's six-gated city,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="16" speaker="">Dardan, and Tymbria, Helias, Chetas, Troien,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="17" speaker="">And Antenorides, with massy staples</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="18" speaker="">And corresponsive and fulfilling bolts,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="19" speaker="">Sperr up the sons of Troy.</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="20" speaker="">Now expectation, tickling skittish spirits,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="21" speaker="">On one and other side, Trojan and Greek,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="22" speaker="">Sets all on hazard: and hither am I come</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="23" speaker="">A prologue arm'd, but not in confidence</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="24" speaker="">Of author's pen or actor's voice, but suited</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="25" speaker="">In like conditions as our argument,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="26" speaker="">To tell you, fair beholders, that our play</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="27" speaker="">Leaps o'er the vaunt and firstlings of those broils,</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="28" speaker="">Beginning in the middle, starting thence away</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="29" speaker="">To what may be digested in a play.</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="30" speaker="">Like or find fault; do as your pleasures are:</line><line act="1" scene="0" line="31" speaker="">Now good or bad, 'tis but the chance of war.</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="1" speaker="TROILUS">Call here my varlet; You vile abominable tents,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="25" speaker="TROILUS">Thus proudly pight upon our Phrygian plains,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="26" speaker="TROILUS">Let Titan rise as early as he dare,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="27" speaker="TROILUS">I'll through and through you! and, thou great-sized coward,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="28" speaker="TROILUS">No space of earth shall sunder our two hates:</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="29" speaker="TROILUS">I'll haunt thee like a wicked conscience still,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="30" speaker="TROILUS">That mouldeth goblins swift as frenzy's thoughts.</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="31" speaker="TROILUS">Strike a free march to Troy! with comfort go:</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="32" speaker="TROILUS">Hope of revenge shall hide our inward woe.</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="33" speaker="PANDARUS">But hear you, hear you!</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="34" speaker="TROILUS">Hence, broker-lackey! ignomy and shame</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="35" speaker="TROILUS">Pursue thy life, and live aye with thy name!</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="36" speaker="PANDARUS">A goodly medicine for my aching bones! O world!</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="37" speaker="PANDARUS">world! world! thus is the poor agent despised!</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="38" speaker="PANDARUS">O traitors and bawds, how earnestly are you set</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="39" speaker="PANDARUS">a-work, and how ill requited! why should our</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="40" speaker="PANDARUS">endeavour be so loved and the performance so loathed?</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="41" speaker="PANDARUS">what verse for it? what instance for it? Let me see:</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="42" speaker="PANDARUS">Full merrily the humble-bee doth sing,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="43" speaker="PANDARUS">Till he hath lost his honey and his sting;</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="44" speaker="PANDARUS">And being once subdued in armed tail,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="45" speaker="PANDARUS">Sweet honey and sweet notes together fail.</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="46" speaker="PANDARUS">Good traders in the flesh, set this in your</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="47" speaker="PANDARUS">painted cloths.</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="48" speaker="PANDARUS">As many as be here of pander's hall,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="49" speaker="PANDARUS">Your eyes, half out, weep out at Pandar's fall;</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="50" speaker="PANDARUS">Or if you cannot weep, yet give some groans,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="51" speaker="PANDARUS">Though not for me, yet for your aching bones.</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="52" speaker="PANDARUS">Brethren and sisters of the hold-door trade,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="53" speaker="PANDARUS">Some two months hence my will shall here be made:</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="54" speaker="PANDARUS">It should be now, but that my fear is this,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="55" speaker="PANDARUS">Some galled goose of Winchester would hiss:</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="56" speaker="PANDARUS">Till then I'll sweat and seek about for eases,</line><line act="5" scene="10" line="57" speaker="PANDARUS">And at that time bequeathe you my diseases.</line>
